QINLoopVPNeutral = {

GolmudBattleSetup = {
	###SETTING UP ATTACKER AND DEFENDERS###
    set_variable = { attacker_total_casualty = 0 }
    set_variable = { defender_total_casualty = 0 }
	set_variable = { BattleAttacker = 0 }
	set_variable = { BattleDefender = 0 }
	set_variable = { BattleRounds = 1 }

	if = {
		limit = {
		    has_country_flag = QIN_VP_Major1
		    has_country_flag = QIN_VP_Major1_Engagement
		}
		set_country_flag = QIN_BOG_01_Attack
		set_variable = { BattleAttacker = QIN_BOG_01_STRENGTH_ALLIED }
		set_variable = { BattleDefender = QIN_BOG_01_STRENGTH_NINGXIA }
        set_variable = { defender_original_count = QIN_BOG_01_STRENGTH_NINGXIA } 
        set_variable = { attacker_original_count = QIN_BOG_01_STRENGTH_ALLIED } 
	}
	else_if = {
	    limit = {
	        has_country_flag = QIN_Ningxia_Attacks_Major1
	    }
		set_country_flag = QIN_BOG_01_Defend
	    set_variable = { BattleAttacker = QIN_BOG_01_STRENGTH_NINGXIA }
	    set_variable = { BattleDefender = QIN_BOG_01_STRENGTH_ALLIED }
        set_variable = { defender_original_count = QIN_BOG_01_STRENGTH_ALLIED } 
        set_variable = { attacker_original_count = QIN_BOG_01_STRENGTH_NINGXIA } 
        set_variable = { Gd = 101 }
	}
	else_if = {

GolmudBattleAttackCalc = {
        set_variable = { attacker_damage = 0 }
        randomize_variable = {
	        var = attacker_damage
	        distribution = binomial
	        min = 75
	        max = 150
        }
        divide_variable = { attacker_damage = 100 }
        multiply_variable = { attacker_damage = BattleAttacker }
        multiply_variable = { attacker_damage = 0.25 }
        set_variable = { atkdmg = attacker_damage }
        round_variable = atkdmg
}
GolmudBattleDefendCalc = {
    #ASSIGNING DEFENSIVE ADVANTAGE TO BATTLE#
    set_variable = { defender_damage_taken = 0 }
    set_variable = { defence_min = 50 }
    set_variable = { defence_max = 150 }

    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = QIN_VP_Major1_Engagement
        }
        add_to_variable = { defence_min = QIN_BOG_01_DEFENSIVE_ADVANTAGE }
        add_to_variable = { defence_max = QIN_BOG_01_DEFENSIVE_ADVANTAGE }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = QIN_VP_Major2_Engagement
        }

GolmudCounterattackCalc = {
        set_variable = { defender_damage = 0 }
        randomize_variable = {
	        var = defender_damage
	        distribution = binomial
	        min = 75
	        max = 150
        }
        divide_variable = { defender_damage = 100 }
        multiply_variable = { defender_damage = BattleDefender }
        multiply_variable = { defender_damage = 0.25 }
        set_variable = { dfddmg = defender_damage }
        round_variable = dfddmg
	    set_variable = { attacker_damage_taken = 0 }
        add_to_variable = { attacker_damage_taken = dfddmg }
        round_variable = attacker_damage_taken
}
GolmudCasualtyCalc = {
    add_to_variable = { 
        var = defender_total_casualty
        value = defender_damage_taken
    }
    add_to_variable = { 
        var = attacker_total_casualty 
        value = attacker_damage_taken
    }

    if = {
        limit = {
            AND = {
                 check_variable = {
	                 var = BattleAttacker
	                 value = attacker_damage_taken
	                 compare = less_than
                 }        
                 check_variable = {
	                 var = BattleAttacker
	                 value = 0
	                 compare = greater_than
                 }
            }
        }
        set_variable = { attacker_damage_taken = BattleAttacker }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
	            var = BattleAttacker
	            value = 0
	            compare = less_than
            }        
        }
        set_variable = { BattleAttacker = 0 }
    }
    else = {
        subtract_from_variable = { BattleAttacker = attacker_damage_taken }  
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            AND = {
                check_variable = {
	                var = BattleDefender
	                value = defender_damage_taken
	                compare = less_than
                }        
                check_variable = {
	                var = BattleDefender
	                value = 0
	                compare = greater_than
                }
            }
        }
        set_variable = { defender_damage_taken = BattleDefender }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
	            var = BattleDefender
	            value = 0
	            compare = less_than
            }
        }
        set_variable = { BattleDefender = 0 }
    }
    else = {
        subtract_from_variable = { BattleDefender = defender_damage_taken }
    }

    divide_variable = {
        var = defender_total_casualty
        value = defender_original_count
    }
    divide_variable = {
        var = attacker_total_casualty
        value = attacker_original_count
    }
    set_variable = { casualty_ratio = 0 }
    set_temp_variable = { defender_total_casualty_temp = defender_total_casualty }
    divide_temp_variable = {
        var = defender_total_casualty_temp
        value = attacker_total_casualty
    }
    set_variable = { casualty_ratio = defender_total_casualty_temp }
}

    set_variable = { GolmudDebug = 200 }
    GolmudBattleAttackCalc = yes
    GolmudBattleDefendCalc = yes
	GolmudCounterattackCalc = yes
	GolmudCasualtyCalc = yes
	GolmudResultCalc = yes
}

}

GolmudReinforce = {
    if = {
        #CHECK IF CONFLICT IS GREATER
        limit = {
            AND = {
            OR = {
    	        check_variable = {
    	            var = QIN_BOG_15_Tension
    	            value = QIN_BOG_01_Tension
    	            compare = greater_than
                }
    	        check_variable = {
    	            var = QIN_BOG_17_Tension
    	            value = QIN_BOG_01_Tension
    	            compare = greater_than
                }
    	        check_variable = {
    	            var = QIN_BOG_30_Tension
    	            value = QIN_BOG_01_Tension
    	            compare = greater_than
                }
    	        check_variable = {
    	            var = QIN_BOG_35_Tension
    	            value = QIN_BOG_01_Tension
    	            compare = greater_than
                }
            }
    	        check_variable = {
    	            var = QIN_BOG_01_STRENGTH_NINGXIA
    	            value = 15
    	            compare = greater_than
                }   
    	        check_variable = {
    	            var = QIN_BOG_01_STRENGTH_ALLIED
    	            value = 0
    	            compare = less_than_or_equals
                }         
            }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { conflict_temp_1 = QIN_BOG_15_Tension }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { conflict_temp_1 = QIN_BOG_01_Tension }
        set_temp_variable = { conflict_temp_2 = QIN_BOG_17_Tension }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { conflict_temp_2 = QIN_BOG_01_Tension }
        set_temp_variable = { conflict_temp_3 = QIN_BOG_30_Tension }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { conflict_temp_3 = QIN_BOG_01_Tension }
        set_temp_variable = { conflict_temp_4 = QIN_BOG_35_Tension }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { conflict_temp_4 = QIN_BOG_01_Tension }
        if = {
            limit = {
                AND = {
    	            check_variable = {
    	                var = conflict_temp_1
    	                value = conflict_temp_2
    	                compare = greater_than_or_equals
                    }
    	            check_variable = {
    	                var = conflict_temp_1
    	                value = conflict_temp_3
    	                compare = greater_than_or_equals
                    }
    	            check_variable = {
    	                var = conflict_temp_1
    	                value = conflict_temp_4
    	                compare = greater_than_or_equals
                    }
                }
            }

QINCalculateSupport = {
    set_variable = { Proposal_Support = 0 }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = NXS_Proposal
        }
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = KMT_Meeting_Proportion_NXS }
        set_temp_variable = { proposal_cck = KMT_Meeting_Proportion_CCK }
        set_temp_variable = { proposal_zxx = KMT_Meeting_Proportion_ZXX }
        divide_temp_variable = { proposal_cck  = 10 }
        divide_temp_variable = {  proposal_zxx = 20 }
        round_temp_variable = proposal_cck
        round_temp_variable = proposal_zxx
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = proposal_cck }
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = proposal_zxx }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = CCK_Proposal
        }
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = KMT_Meeting_Proportion_CCK }
        set_temp_variable = { proposal_nxs = KMT_Meeting_Proportion_NXS }
        set_temp_variable = { proposal_zxx = KMT_Meeting_Proportion_ZXX }
        divide_temp_variable = { proposal_nxs  = 15 }
        divide_temp_variable = {  proposal_zxx = 15 }
        round_temp_variable = proposal_nxs
        round_temp_variable = proposal_zxx
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = proposal_nxs }
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = proposal_zxx }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = ZXX_Proposal
        }
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = KMT_Meeting_Proportion_ZXX }
        set_temp_variable = { proposal_cck = KMT_Meeting_Proportion_CCK }
        set_temp_variable = { proposal_nxs = KMT_Meeting_Proportion_NXS }
        divide_temp_variable = { proposal_cck  = 10 }
        divide_temp_variable = {  proposal_nxs = 20 }
        round_temp_variable = proposal_cck
        round_temp_variable = proposal_nxs
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = proposal_cck }
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = proposal_nxs }
    }

    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = proposalboost3
        }
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = 25 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = proposalboost2
        }        
        set_temp_variable = { proposal2mult = 15 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { proposal2mult = proposalboost2_multiplier }
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = proposal2mult }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = proposalboost1
        }        
        set_temp_variable = { proposal1mult = 5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { proposal1mult = proposalboost1_multiplier }
        add_to_variable = { Proposal_Support = proposal1mult }
    }
}

QIN_ProposalClearFlags = {
    clr_country_flag = ZXX_Proposal
    clr_country_flag = CCK_Proposal
    clr_country_flag = NXS_Proposal
    clr_country_flag = proposalboost3
    clr_country_flag = proposalboost2
    clr_country_flag = proposalboost1
}

QINDecidePresident = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            AND = {
                check_variable = {
                	var = KMT_Chen_Support
                	value = KMT_Wang_Support
                	compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
                check_variable = {
                	var = KMT_Chen_Support
                	value = KMT_Chiang_Support
                	compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
            }
        }
        set_country_flag = Chen_Victory
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            AND = {
                check_variable = {
                	var = KMT_Wang_Support
                	value = KMT_Chen_Support
                	compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
                check_variable = {
                	var = KMT_Wang_Support
                	value = KMT_Chiang_Support
                	compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
            }
        }
        set_country_flag = Wang_Victory
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            AND = {
                check_variable = {
                	var = KMT_Chiang_Support
                	value = KMT_Chen_Support
                	compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
                check_variable = {
                	var = KMT_Chiang_Support
                	value = KMT_Wang_Support
                	compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
            }
        }
        set_country_flag = Chiang_Victory
    }
}
QINDecidepresidency = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = Chen_Victory
        }
        complete_national_focus = third_revolution
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = Wang_Victory
        }
        complete_national_focus = for_democracy
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = Chiang_Victory
        }
        complete_national_focus = ten_more_years
    }
}

Update_pie_chart_QIN = {
    #WOW NEW PIE
	##KMT
	set_variable = { BOG_NEUTRAL_pie_start = 0 }
	set_variable = { BOG_NEUTRAL_pie_end = BOG_NEUTRAL^VP_Token }
    set_variable = { BOG_NEUTRAL_pie_frame = BOG_NEUTRAL_pie_start } 
	round_variable = BOG_NEUTRAL_pie_frame 
	multiply_variable = { BOG_NEUTRAL_pie_frame = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BOG_NEUTRAL_pie_frame = BOG_NEUTRAL_pie_end }
    
	##CCP
	set_variable = { BOG_NINGXIA_pie_start = BOG_NEUTRAL_pie_end }
	set_variable = { BOG_NINGXIA_pie_end = BOG_NINGXIA_pie_start }
	add_to_variable = { BOG_NINGXIA_pie_end = BOG_NINGXIA^VP_Token }
    set_variable = { BOG_NINGXIA_pie_frame = BOG_NINGXIA_pie_start } 
	round_variable = BOG_NINGXIA_pie_frame
	multiply_variable = { BOG_NINGXIA_pie_frame = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BOG_NINGXIA_pie_frame = BOG_NINGXIA_pie_end }
	
	##QINGHAI
	set_variable = { BOG_QINGHAI_pie_start = BOG_NINGXIA_pie_end }
	set_variable = { BOG_QINGHAI_pie_end = BOG_QINGHAI_pie_start }
	add_to_variable = { BOG_QINGHAI_pie_end = BOG_QINGHAI^VP_Token }
    set_variable = { BOG_QINGHAI_pie_frame = BOG_QINGHAI_pie_start } 
	round_variable = BOG_QINGHAI_pie_frame
	multiply_variable = { BOG_QINGHAI_pie_frame = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BOG_QINGHAI_pie_frame = BOG_QINGHAI_pie_end }

    ##NINGXIA
	set_variable = { BOG_CCP_pie_start = BOG_QINGHAI_pie_end }
	set_variable = { BOG_CCP_pie_end = BOG_CCP_pie_start }
	add_to_variable = { BOG_CCP_pie_end = BOG_CCP^VP_Token }
    set_variable = { BOG_CCP_pie_frame = BOG_CCP_pie_start } 
	round_variable = BOG_CCP_pie_frame
	multiply_variable = { BOG_CCP_pie_frame = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BOG_CCP_pie_frame = BOG_CCP_pie_end }
    
	##NEUTRAL
	set_variable = { BOG_KMT_pie_start = BOG_CCP_pie_end }
    set_variable = { BOG_KMT_pie_frame = BOG_KMT_pie_start } 
	round_variable = BOG_KMT_pie_frame
	multiply_variable = { BOG_KMT_pie_frame = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BOG_KMT_pie_frame = 100 } # last one so make it 100
}
